---------------------------BRF181_MAPPING_PROCEDURE-------------

create or replace PROCEDURE "BRF181_MAPPING_PROCEDURE" (REPORT_DATE VARCHAR2) 

IS 
  V_REPORT_DATE DATE := To_date (REPORT_DATE, 'DD-MM-YYYY'); 
BEGIN

report_addl_criteria_1 = 'ROW496B' WHERE CONSTITUTION_CODE IN ('11599');
COMMIT;

--ROW498A

report_addl_criteria_1 = 'ROW498A' WHERE CONSTITUTION_CODE IN ('11509');
COMMIT;


--ROW498B
UPDATE   brf181_mapping_table SET  REPORT_NAME_1 ='BRF181', REPORT_LABEL_1 = 'ROW498',
report_addl_criteria_1 = 'ROW498B' WHERE CONSTITUTION_CODE IN ('11599');
COMMIT;

COMMIT;
END;


--------------------BRF181_DETAIL_PROCEDURE------------------------

create or replace PROCEDURE BRF181_DETAIL_PROCEDURE (REPORT_DATE DATE)
IS
  V_REPORT_DATE DATE := To_date (REPORT_DATE, 'DD-MM-YYYY'); 
   V_FROM_DATE dATE :=  ADD_MONTHS (LAST_DAY (REPORT_DATE), -1) + 1;
BEGIN


delete from BRF181_DETAILTABLE where report_date = V_REPORT_DATE;
Commit;


insert into BRF181_DETAILTABLE
( foracid, cust_id, ACCT_NAME,REPORT_DATE, REPORT_LABEL_1,REPORT_NAME_1,REPORT_ADDL_CRITERIA_1)
SELECT  foracid, cust_id, ACCT_NAME,REPORT_DATE,REPORT_LABEL_1,REPORT_NAME_1,REPORT_ADDL_CRITERIA_1 FROM 
brf181_mapping_table where report_date = '30-JUN-2023' AND REPORT_LABEL_1 IS NOT NULL ;


COMMIT;

MERGE INTO BRF181_DETAILTABLE M
USING (
    SELECT   b.REPORT_LABEL_1,b.cust_id,b.foracid
    FROM brf181_mapping_table b
    JOIN BRF181_DETAILTABLE a ON a.foracid = b.foracid
    WHERE a.report_date = V_REPORT_DATE
) S
ON (M.foracid = S.foracid)
WHEN MATCHED THEN UPDATE
SET M.REPORT_LABEL_1 = S.REPORT_LABEL_1
WHERE M.report_date = V_REPORT_DATE;
COMMIT;

MERGE INTO BRF181_DETAILTABLE M
USING (
    SELECT   b.nre_status,b.cust_id,b.foracid
    FROM brf181_mapping_table b
    JOIN BRF181_DETAILTABLE a ON a.foracid = b.foracid
    WHERE a.report_date = V_REPORT_DATE
) S
ON (M.foracid = S.foracid)
WHEN MATCHED THEN UPDATE
SET M.NRE_FLG = S.nre_status
WHERE M.report_date = V_REPORT_DATE;
COMMIT;


END;

BEGIN BRF_181_A_PROCEDURE('30-JUN-2023'); 
END;

DELETE FROM BRF181_DETAILTABLE

SELECT * FROM BRF181B_SUMMARYTABLE
